< review>
I always get the enchiladas meal for $6.00- and it is the best six dollars you will spend! The servers are always nice, and happy to give you refills of the freshly made salsa they make in-house. There is always a free appetizer offered, as well. The enchiladas plate is huge and comes with rice and beans. The fact that they change the appetizer and the salsa every day astounds me, especially since I have enjoyed everything they have offered. My favorite place in Pilsen, hands down, for Mexican.<//review>

< review>
I registered to attend Scrum master training through this company.  Although they did not conduct the actual training, I will say they have very good customer service.  They responded immediately to my questions during the registration process and communicated effectively through emails to ensure I was set for the training.
Why only four stars?  I can only give four stars because after I registered, I learned that military veterans who are paying out of pocket to attend the training could get 50% off their registration fee.  When I registered, I was given a military discount.  However, upon reading further, I asked if I could be reimbursed for the difference.  I was told that they did not offer the 50% discount, so I shared the screenshot from their website.

This is just bad customer service.  I am ok with offering a 25% discount, or a 50% discount, or no discount at all for veterans, but if the site indicates that they provide a 50% discount, the organization should honor that advertisement.  These courses are expensive and some veterans can really benefit (and need) the savings.  My recommendation is that all the organizations who are involved in the registration process get on the same page to eliminate confusion and frustration.< /review>

None</Pictures>

I am very sad to have to post this but it is a safety issue. I have lived in Chico my whole life and have seen this park at its best and unfortunately it is at its worst right now. There are numerous illegal encampments that the City is doing absolutely nothing about. I have done volunteer clean ups in lower Bidwell park and the amount of trash, human fecal waste and drug paraphernalia is off the charts. Many years ago it was a safe place to enjoy with your family and friends. Now it is not a safe place to be at all. The criminal element is everywhere. <userid>108989806260087996728</userid><user_name>James Griffith< /user_name><date>1550583507698</date>< rate>
5</rate>
< text>
The 3600 acre park is one of the largest municipal parks in the U-S. It stretches for miles from close to Chico's downtown (One Mile Area) to well up into the foothills miles out of town where nude swimming is tolerated in the cold waters of Chico creek. The park offers miles of hiking, biking and horseback riding trails and paths some of which are paved while others are dirt and more suited for trail bikes. A portion of the natural creek has been cemented and dammed to create a large area for swimming safely in the flowing creek waters. Bidwell Park is so beautiful it was used as a substitute for the English countryside the 1938 action classic, "The Adventures of Robin Hood" starring Erroll Flynn highlighted by the famous duel between Robin Hood and Little John staged over Chico Creek which is at the center of the park and provides water for the hundreds of stately mature California oak trees and dozens of other plants that make the park so special. If you visit Chico and don't spend time in the park, you are missing the one attraction that makes Chico truly unique.</text>

<text>My boyfriend took me here on our second date. We came for a picnic in September when it still felt like July. We ate under the trees, watched other people seek respite from the heat in the shade, the kids swim in the natural pool, and enjoyed the overall languid, California summer feel.

The park is a great space, with a lot of different options for different activities--swimming, walking/running, lounging, you could even set up a slack line between any of the large oak trees if you were so inclined.

A beautiful space that I now have wonderful memories of...go create some of your own!<//text>< pics>

One of the largest municipal parks in the state. Lower park is more "civilized" Paved roadway, large pool at 1 mile 6 mile loop open to cars. Upper park is more natural, lots of hiking trails. The north side is off leash for dogs. The lower park is only off leash to 8:30 in the morning.<//text>
